/Pg 8 0 R /K [15] >> endobj 191 0 obj << /Type /StructElem /S /P /ActualText (wpwizardguide.com) /Pg 8 0 R /K [18] >> endobj 192 0 obj << /Type /StructElem /S /H1 /T (Overview of WordPress) /E (Overview of WordPress) /Pg 9 0 R /K [0] >> endobj 193 0 obj << /Type /StructElem /S /P /ActualText (WordPress is an immensely popular content management system \(CMS\) that empowers users to create and manage websites with ease. Initially launched in 2003 as a simple blogging platform, WordPress has evolved into a versatile tool that powers over 40% of all websites on the internet. This platform stands out for its user-friendly interface, extensive customization options through themes and plugins, and a robust community of developers and users who continuously contribute to its growth and accessibility.
